I have stayed in many hotels in the front mountain. This time I chose Shanzun Hotel. I feel that I can live here directly when I come here. The environment of the hotel is very good, with a garden-style design, pavilions and towers scattered in an orderly manner. The entire hotel is much larger than I imagined. There is a private trail behind it for walking, which is really a must, and the scenery is very good. The service of the hotel is also very considerate. It can be said that it is the most considerate service I have felt since the resumption of travel last year. There is nothing to complain about in all aspects. We booked a private soup room. The room area is quite large, and there is a terrace outside. It is very comfortable for a family of three to live in. The breakfast of the hotel is also great. Although the restaurant is not large, it has a full range of categories, both Chinese and Western. What I like most is that they also prepare Yeerba, brown sugar fermented glutinous rice flour and bean curd, which feels very distinctive and tastes very good. I will definitely come again in the future. Thank you for the excellent service provided by the hotel service staff during our two days of stay.

name:Z‚Äçz‚Äçz‚Äç0‚Äç.‚Äço
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Friends
info:4 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 2, 2024
msg:I went to Qingcheng Mountain with my friends and chose this hotel after reading online recommendations.
This hotel is the best among the Garden Hotels I have stayed in. I have rarely taken the initiative to write reviews for the hotel, but this hotel is worth it.

To be honest, there are many good hotels in Qingcheng Mountain, but there are really few that have such a large area and private forest as Qingcheng Mountain Zun.

The hotel is like a huge nursing home. Every day when you get up, you can hear the chirping of birds outside. When you go out, you can see the garden landscape. When you walk on the road, you can smell the fragrance of various plants. After finishing the buffet in the morning, it is very comfortable to walk in the private garden. There are also little squirrels on the road.

We booked a private bath room and the front desk upgraded it to a room with a garden view. There is a jacuzzi in the yard. There is no need to wait for hot water from the faucet in the room. The room staff are very polite and attentive. However, because the room floor is low and the hotel is well greened, bugs will come in when the weather is hot.

The guest rooms in the hotel are divided into several buildings. The hotel lobby is also a separate building. The decoration design is very grand and high-end. Although the lobby and guest rooms are not in the same place, the front desk staff is very efficient and answers calls to the front desk in seconds every time. And can quickly arrange room service and shuttle bus

However, one troublesome point is that the location of the hotel is relatively remote. It is recommended to drive here (it is normal for such a large garden landscape to be in a remote location). The shuttle service in the hotel is very convenient. Each building has a direct telephone number to the switchboard. You can get through when you get up and call for a taxi. The drivers are very friendly and have a comprehensive understanding of the hotel. They can also introduce us to the various facilities and business hours of the hotel.

The breakfast buffet was quite satisfactory. The service staff were polite and prompt.
All in all it was a good experience
